It is not difficult to know the discussion on the drop of calls from the Ministry of Communications to the PMO and corporate meetings on call drop Is that the problem of bad mobile network is not so big that it requires political consensus or consumers need to give subsidy on telephone bill instead of poor service

 The basic principle of mobile networks is that the lower the frequency band, the more comfortable communication will be
 yahi vajah he ki haal main jab spectrum (frequency) kaa aavanton hua to zyada hode 900 megahatrj ke band ke liye thi
 But there is less space in the good frequency band, so more companies try to achieve this

 desh main kareeb 96 karod mobile upabhoktaaon ko seva dene ke liye 5
 There are 5 lakh towers
 achche yani nichle frequency band ke liye kam tower chahie lekin 3ji or 4ji yani oonche band kii sarvice ke liye zyada toweron kii jarurat hoti he
 In examining the role of government and companies in the light of these basic facts, one will realize that the problem is not huge, but the matter is of resolve, seriousness, lack of coordination and reluctance to put pressure on companies, which has made India's mobile revolution Has made an astringent sabase pehle toweron kii kami ko lete hai
